############################
# ARTISTS SCRPITED EFFECTS #
############################

############################################################################

#All Academics (and Special Characters) should have a variable assigned to the character:
# mr_is_composer_var	-->	Composer
# mr_is_writer_var		-->	Writer
# mr_is_painter_var		-->	Painter
# mr_is_architect_var	-->	Architect

######Artistic Progress######

#This effect is used to add the monthly Artistic Progress
artists_monthly_artistic_progress_effect = {
	if = { #Effect only gets executed if there is either an Arts Academy or an Opera
		limit = {
			any_scope_building = {
				OR = {
					is_building_type = building_arts_academy
					is_building_type = building_elgar_opera
				}
				level >= 1
			}
		}

		#Set up
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_variable = artists_artistic_progress_var } }
			set_variable = {
				name = artists_artistic_progress_var
				value = 0
			}
		}

		#Add monthly variable to the total variable
		if = {
			limit = { monthly_artistic_progress_gain_value > 0 }
			change_variable = {
				name = artists_artistic_progress_var
				add = monthly_artistic_progress_gain_value
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = { var:artists_artistic_progress_var >= 1000 }
			change_variable = {
				name = artists_artistic_progress_var
				subtract = 1000
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_variable = artists_promote_composer_active_var }
				trigger_event = {
					id = artists.51
					popup = yes
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_variable = artists_promote_writer_active_var }
				trigger_event = {
					id = artists.52
					popup = yes
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_variable = artists_promote_painter_active_var }
				trigger_event = {
					id = artists.53
					popup = yes
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_variable = artists_promote_architect_active_var }
				trigger_event = {
					id = artists.54
					popup = yes
				}
			}
			else = {
				random_list = {
					10 = {
						trigger_event = {
							id = artists.51
							popup = yes
						}
						modifier = {
							if = {
								limit = { elgar_has_composer_no_tooltip_trigger = yes }
								add = -7
							}
						}
					}
					10 = {
						trigger_event = {
							id = artists.52
							popup = yes
						}
						modifier = {
							if = {
								limit = { manzoni_has_writer_no_tooltip = yes }
								add = -7
							}
						}
					}
					10 = {
						trigger_event = {
							id = artists.53
							popup = yes
						}
						modifier = {
							if = {
								limit = { klimt_has_painter_no_tooltip = yes }
								add = -7
							}
						}
					}
					10 = {
						trigger_event = {
							id = artists.54
							popup = yes
						}
						modifier = {
							if = {
								limit = { gaudi_has_architect_no_tooltip_trigger = yes }
								add = -7
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#Effect to add $AMOUNT$ Artistic Progress
artists_add_x_artistic_progress = {
	# Amount = amount of Artistic Progress to add
	save_temporary_scope_value_as = { #This is used to display the amount in the tooltip
		name = academy_progress_amount
		value = $AMOUNT$
	}

	#This part is used to display an accurate tooltip (Gain, loss, etc.)
	if = { #Negative Plural Tooltip if $AMOUNT$ is negative
		limit = { $AMOUNT$ < -1 }
		custom_tooltip = artists_add_x_artistic_progress_minus_x_tt
	}
	if = { #Negative Singular Tooltip if $AMOUNT$ is negative
		limit = { $AMOUNT$ = -1 }
		custom_tooltip = artists_add_x_artistic_progress_minus_1_tt
	}
	if = { #Neutral Tooltip if $AMOUNT$ is 0
		limit = { $AMOUNT$ = 0 }
		custom_tooltip = artists_add_x_artistic_progress_0_tt
	}
	if = { #Positive Plural Tooltip if $AMOUNT$ is positive
		limit = { $AMOUNT$ = 1 }
		custom_tooltip = artists_add_x_artistic_progress_plus_1_tt
	}
	if = { #Positive Plural Tooltip if $AMOUNT$ is positive
		limit = { $AMOUNT$ > 1 }
		custom_tooltip = artists_add_x_artistic_progress_plus_x_tt
	}

	#This part adds the AMOUNT of Artistic Progress
	if = { #Fallback if the variable does not exist yet
		limit = {
			NOT = {
				has_variable = artists_artistic_progress_var
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = artists_artistic_progress_var
			value = 0
		}
	}
	change_variable = {
		name = artists_artistic_progress_var
		add = $AMOUNT$
	}
}

#This effect is used to set up the list of travelling composers
artists_set_up_travelling_composer_list_effect = {
	clear_global_variable_list = mr_travelling_composer_global_list
	ordered_character_in_void = {
		max = 1000
		order_by = var:elgar_composer_experience
		check_range_bounds = no

		limit = {
			has_variable = mr_is_travelling_composer_var
		}
		add_to_global_variable_list = {
			name = mr_travelling_composer_global_list
			target = this
		}
	}
}

#This effect is used to remove the travelling composers as there shouldn't be too many.
artists_remove_travelling_composer_from_void_effect = {
	if = {
		#This part is used to limit the effect to only one country
		limit = {
			NOT = { has_global_variable = artists_travelling_composer_remove_global_var }
		}
		set_global_variable = {
			name = artists_travelling_composer_remove_global_var
			days = 15
		}

		#This is used to keep track of the current number
		set_local_variable = {
			name = current_number
			value = 0
		}
		
		#This part gets the travelling composers ordered by experience.
		# The Composers that are not historical and are over the limit will be deleted.
		ordered_character_in_void = {
			limit = { has_variable = mr_is_travelling_composer_var }
			order_by = var:elgar_composer_experience
			max = 1000
			check_range_bounds = no

			change_local_variable = {
				name = current_number
				add = 1
			}

			if = {
				limit = {
					local_var:current_number > 20
					is_historical = no
				}
				free_character_from_void = no
			}
		}
	}
}

#This effect is used to remove the independent painters as there shouldn't be too many.
artists_remove_independent_painter_from_void_effect = {
	if = {
		#This part is used to limit the effect to only one country
		limit = {
			NOT = { has_global_variable = artists_independent_painter_remove_global_var }
		}
		set_global_variable = {
			name = artists_independent_painter_remove_global_var
			days = 15
		}

		#This is used to keep track of the current number
		set_local_variable = {
			name = current_number
			value = 0
		}
		
		#This part gets the independent artists ordered by experience.
		# The Composers that are not historical and are over the limit will be deleted.
		ordered_character_in_void = {
			limit = { has_variable = mr_is_independent_painter }
			order_by = var:klimt_painter_experience
			max = 1000
			check_range_bounds = no

			change_local_variable = {
				name = current_number
				add = 1
			}

			if = {
				limit = {
					local_var:current_number > 20
					is_historical = no
				}
				free_character_from_void = no
			}
		}
	}
}

#This effect is used to set up the list of local writers
artists_set_up_local_writer_list_effect = {
	clear_variable_list = mr_local_writers_list
	ordered_character_in_void = {
		max = 1000
		order_by = var:manzoni_writer_experience
		check_range_bounds = no

		limit = {
			has_variable = mr_is_local_writer_var
			var:mr_is_local_writer_var = {
				this = root
			}
		}
		root = {
			add_to_variable_list = {
				name = mr_local_writers_list
				target = prev
			}
		}
	}
}

#This effect is used to set up the list of independent painters
artists_set_up_independent_painter_list_effect = {
	clear_global_variable_list = mr_independent_painter_global_list
	ordered_character_in_void = {
		max = 1000
		order_by = var:klimt_painter_experience
		check_range_bounds = no

		limit = {
			has_variable = mr_is_independent_painter
		}
		add_to_global_variable_list = {
			name = mr_independent_painter_global_list
			target = this
		}
	}
}

######COMPOSER######

#This effect kills the current composer
# !!! Change stuff in both of the following effects !!!
kill_composer_effect = {
	var:elgar_composer_var = {
		free_character_from_void = no
	}

	remove_variable = elgar_composer_var
	hidden_effect = {
		elgar_remove_composer_modifier_effect = yes
		remove_modifier = elgar_conductor_exhausted_modifier
	}
}
#This Effect retires the current Composer
# Use "set_retirement_variable_effect" in the immediate effect when using this effect.
retire_composer_effect = {
	custom_tooltip = {
		text = retire_composer_effect_tt

		var:elgar_composer_var = {
			free_character_from_void = no
		}
	}

	remove_variable = elgar_composer_var
	elgar_remove_composer_modifier_effect = yes
	remove_modifier = elgar_conductor_exhausted_modifier
}

#This effect makes the current composer a travelling Composer
set_composer_travelling_composer_effect = {
	if = {
		limit = { has_variable = elgar_composer_var }

		custom_tooltip = {
			text = elgar_set_composer_travelling_composer_tt
	
			var:elgar_composer_var = {
				elgar_set_composer_travelling_composer = yes
			}
		
			remove_variable = elgar_composer_var
		}
	}
}

# Creates a new Composer without losing the old one
#This one was a little harder as the scope was only valid in the random_list
#Therefore a Variable is set to save the scope again. then gets deleted
create_new_composer_effect = {
	random_list = {
		#Historical Characters
		200 = { #Anton Bruckner, Austria
			trigger = {
				NOT = { has_global_variable = mr_bruckner_created_global_var }
				has_state_in_state_region = STATE_AUSTRIA
				country_average_cultural_acceptance = {
					target = cu:south_german
					value >= acceptance_status_3
				}
				game_date < 1879.9.4 #Age 55
				year >= 1855 #Worked in Linz
			}
			create_character = {
				template = mr_aus_bruckner_anton_character_template
				save_scope_as = elgar_new_composer_scope
			}
			scope:elgar_new_composer_scope = {
				set_variable = mr_is_composer_var
				set_variable = mr_no_headgear_var
				composer_experience_set_up_effect = yes
				place_character_in_void = 1200
			}

			set_variable = {
				name = elgar_new_composer_var
				value = scope:elgar_new_composer_scope
			}

			set_global_variable = mr_bruckner_created_global_var
		}
		100 = { #Simon Sechter, Austria
			trigger = {
				NOT = { has_global_variable = mr_sechter_created_global_var }
				has_state_in_state_region = STATE_AUSTRIA
				country_average_cultural_acceptance = {
					target = cu:south_german
					value >= acceptance_status_3
				}
				game_date < 1843.10.11 #Age 55
				year >= 1804 #Moved to Vienna
			}
			create_character = {
				template = mr_aus_sechter_simon_character_template
				save_scope_as = elgar_new_composer_scope
			}
			scope:elgar_new_composer_scope = {
				set_variable = mr_is_composer_var
				set_variable = mr_no_headgear_var
				set_variable = mr_female_glasses_var
				composer_experience_set_up_effect = yes
				place_character_in_void = 1200
			}

			set_variable = {
				name = elgar_new_composer_var

						}
						if = {
							limit = { has_law = law_type:law_women_in_the_workplace }
							add = 7
						}
						if = {
							limit = { has_law = law_type:law_womens_suffrage }
							add = 14
						}
					}

							limit = { has_law = law_type:law_women_in_the_workplace }

							limit = { has_law = law_type:law_womens_suffrage }
							add = -14
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

		save_scope_as = elgar_new_composer_scope
		set_start_composer_stats_effect = yes
	}

# Set new Composer as official Composer
elgar_set_new_composer_as_composer_effect = {
	custom_tooltip = {
		text = elgar_replace_composer_with_new_composer_tt

		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = elgar_composer_var
			}

			#Sends the old Painter to the independent Painters
			var:elgar_composer_var = {
				elgar_set_composer_travelling_composer = yes
			}
		}

		set_variable = {
			name = elgar_composer_var
			value = scope:elgar_new_composer_scope
		}

		#Removes ongoing projects
		set_variable = {
			name = elgar_stopped_composing_remover_var
			days = 5
		}
		remove_modifier = elgar_conductor_exhausted_modifier

		remove_variable = elgar_new_composer_var

		#Adds the Default Action
		add_journal_entry = {
			type = je_elgar_composer_composing
		}
	}
}

# Remove new Composer
elgar_remove_new_composer_effect = {
	scope:elgar_new_composer_scope = {
		free_character_from_void = no
	}

	remove_variable = elgar_new_composer_var
}

#Sets Composer as Travelling composer
elgar_set_composer_travelling_composer = {
	remove_variable = mr_is_composer_var
	set_variable = mr_is_travelling_composer_var

	#Is used to prevent a country from getting that composer immediately afterwards
	set_variable = {
		name = elgar_composer_unavailable_for_this_var
		value = root
		years = 5
	}

	#Starts the Composer travelling counter
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { has_variable = mr_travelling_composer_year_counter_var }
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = mr_travelling_composer_year_counter_var
			value = 0
		}
	}
	#Adds the Composer to the Travelling Composer Pool
	add_to_global_variable_list = {
		name = mr_travelling_composer_global_list
		target = this
	}
}

#This effect makes the new composer a travelling Composer
set_new_composer_travelling_composer_effect = {
	custom_tooltip = {
		text = elgar_set_new_composer_travelling_composer_tt

		scope:elgar_new_composer_scope = {
			elgar_set_composer_travelling_composer = yes
		}
	
		remove_variable = elgar_new_composer_var
	}
}

# Used to set up the Experience of a character 
composer_experience_set_up_effect = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = {
				has_variable = elgar_composer_experience
			}
		}
		#Age: 2 Reputation for each year older than 25
		if = {
			limit = {
				age > 25
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = elgar_composer_experience
				value = age
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = elgar_composer_experience
				add = -25
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = elgar_composer_experience
				multiply = 2
			}
		}
		else = {
			set_variable = {
				name = elgar_composer_experience
				value = 0
			}
		}
		#Random Reputation factor
		set_local_variable = {
			name = random_amount_local_var
			value = { 25 50 }
		}
		change_variable = {
			name = elgar_composer_experience
			add = local_var:random_amount_local_var
		}
		change_variable = {
			name = elgar_composer_experience
			add = artists_composer_experience_set_up_value
		}
		if = { #Adds the Famous Composer Trait if Experience is above 500
			limit = {
				var:elgar_composer_experience >= 500
				NOT = {
					has_trait = elgar_great_composer
				}
			}
			remove_trait = elgar_composer
			add_trait = elgar_great_composer
			owner = {
				elgar_add_great_composer_count_effect = yes
			}
		}
	}
	set_variable = {
		name = elgar_composer_num_compositions_var
		value = 0
	}
	set_variable = {
		name = elgar_composer_num_seasons_var
		value = 0
	}
	set_variable = {
		name = elgar_composer_num_tours_var
		value = 0
	}
	set_variable = {
		name = elgar_composer_num_masterworks_var
		value = 0
	}
}

#Composer Experience gain
composer_experience_gain_effect = { #adds XP to the Composer
	# Amount = amount of XP to add
	save_temporary_scope_value_as = { #This is used to display the amount in the tooltip
		name = xp_amount
		value = $AMOUNT$
	}

	if = {
		limit = {
			has_variable = elgar_composer_var #should only add experience if there actually is a Composer
		}
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = elgar_composer_experience_gain_tt
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						var:elgar_composer_var = { #Fallback to make sure there are no errors if the Composer does not have the variable yet
							has_variable = elgar_composer_experience
						}
					}
				}
				var:elgar_composer_var = { #Sets the experience in case it was not set yet
					composer_experience_set_up_effect = yes
				}
			}
			var:elgar_composer_var = {
				change_variable = {
					name = elgar_composer_experience
					add = $AMOUNT$
				}
				clamp_variable = {
					name = elgar_composer_experience
					min = 0
					max = 500
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:elgar_composer_var = {
					var:elgar_composer_experience >= 500
					NOT = {
						has_trait = elgar_great_composer
					}
				}
			}
			trigger_event = {
				id = artists.101
				popup = yes
			}
			elgar_add_great_composer_count_effect = yes
			hidden_effect = {
				var:elgar_composer_var = {
					remove_trait = elgar_composer
					add_trait = elgar_great_composer
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#Void Composer Experience gain
void_composer_experience_gain_effect = { #adds XP to the Composer
	# Amount = amount of XP to add
	save_temporary_scope_value_as = { #This is used to display the amount in the tooltip
		name = xp_amount
		value = $AMOUNT$
	}
	save_scope_as = elgar_travelling_composer_scope

	custom_tooltip = {
		text = elgar_void_composer_experience_gain_tt
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_variable = elgar_composer_experience }
			}
			composer_experience_set_up_effect = yes
		}
		change_variable = {
			name = elgar_composer_experience
			add = $AMOUNT$
		}
		clamp_variable = {
			name = elgar_composer_experience
			min = 0
			max = 500
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { var:elgar_composer_experience < 0 }
		set_variable = {
			name = elgar_composer_experience
			value = 0
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			var:elgar_composer_experience >= 500
			NOT = {
				has_trait = elgar_great_composer
			}
		}
		remove_trait = elgar_composer
		add_trait = elgar_great_composer
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			var:elgar_composer_experience > 500
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = elgar_composer_experience
			value = 500
		}
	}
}

#Effect used to set the cost of the travelling composer
#Use it in the character scope with root being a country.
elgar_travelling_composer_character_set_up_cost_effect = {
	root = {
		add_treasury = {
			if = {
				limit = { prev.var:elgar_composer_experience > 0 }
				value = prev.var:elgar_composer_experience
				divide = 5
				multiply = money_amount_multiplier_small
				max = {
					value = prev.var:elgar_composer_experience
					multiply = 10000
				}
				multiply = -1
			}
			else = {
				value = 1
				divide = 5
				multiply = money_amount_multiplier_small
				max = 100000
				multiply = -1
			}
		}
	}
}

#This effect gives special historical characters 250-350 reputation when created
set_historical_composer_experience_effect = {
	set_variable = {
		name = elgar_composer_experience
		value = { 250 350 }
	}
	set_variable = {
		name = elgar_composer_num_compositions_var
		value = { 5 20 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_trait = elgar_conductor
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = elgar_composer_num_seasons_var
			value = { 1 3 }
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_trait = elgar_virtuoso
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = elgar_composer_num_tours_var
			value = { 2 4 }
		}
	}
	else = {
		set_variable = {
			name = elgar_composer_num_tours_var
			value = { 0 2 }
		}
	}
}

#This effect gives starter characters some random stats
set_start_composer_stats_effect = {
	set_variable = {
		name = elgar_composer_num_compositions_var
		value = { 1 7 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_trait = elgar_conductor
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = elgar_composer_num_seasons_var
			value = { 0 1 }
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_trait = elgar_virtuoso
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = elgar_composer_num_tours_var
			value = { 1 3 }
		}
	}
	else = {
		set_variable = {
			name = elgar_composer_num_tours_var
			value = { 0 2 }
		}
	}
}

######Writer######

#This effect kills the current writer
kill_writer_effect = {
	var:manzoni_writer_var = {
		free_character_from_void = no
	}

	remove_variable = manzoni_writer_var
}

#This effect makes the current writer a local writer
set_writer_local_writer_effect = {
	if = {
		limit = { has_variable = manzoni_writer_var }

		custom_tooltip = {
			text = manzoni_set_writer_local_writer_tt
	
			var:manzoni_writer_var = {
				remove_variable = mr_is_writer_var
				set_variable = {
					name = mr_is_local_writer_var
					value = root
				}
			}
		
			remove_variable = manzoni_writer_var
			artists_set_up_local_writer_list_effect = yes
		}
	}
}

#This effect makes the local writer an agitator
set_mr_character_to_agitator_character_scope_effect = {
	custom_tooltip = {
		text = set_mr_character_to_agitator_character_scope_effect_tt

		#Frees the character from the void.
		free_character_from_void = yes

		#Removes all roles and adds the agitator role.
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_role = agitator }
			}
			add_character_role = agitator
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_role = general
			}
			remove_character_role = general
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_role = admiral
			}
			remove_character_role = admiral
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_role = politician
			}
			set_as_interest_group_leader = no
			remove_character_role = politician
		}

		#If this is the national writer, the variable containing him gets removed.
		if = {
			limit = {
				root.var:manzoni_writer_var ?= this
			}
			#Removes writer character variable
			remove_variable = mr_is_writer_var
			
			#Removes the writer variable
			root = {
				remove_variable = manzoni_writer_var
			}
		}

		#If the writer is a local writer they get removed from the pool
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = mr_is_local_writer_var
			}
			#Removes the local writer character variable
			remove_variable = mr_is_local_writer_var

			#Removes the local writer from the list
			root = {
				remove_list_variable = {
					name = mr_local_writers_list
					target = prev
				}
			}
		}

		#If this is a painter the variable gets removed
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = mr_is_painter_var
			}
			#Removes the local writer character variable
			remove_variable = mr_is_painter_var
			
			#Removes the painter variable
			root = {
				remove_variable = klimt_painter_var
			}
		}
	}
}

#This effect makes a normal character become a local writer
set_character_as_local_writer_character_scope_effect = {
	custom_tooltip = {
		save_scope_as = wannabe_writer_scope
		text = set_character_as_local_writer_scope_effect_tt
		#In case you decide any character should become a writer this gives them the base trait
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_trait = literary }
			}
			add_trait = literary
		}
		#Sets the specialization Trait
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOR = {
					has_trait = manzoni_writer_fiction
					has_trait = manzoni_writer_poet
					has_trait = manzoni_writer_playwright
					has_trait = manzoni_writer_non_fiction
				}
			}
			mr_trait_generation_writer_specialization_effect = yes
		}
		#Sets the Genre trait
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_trait = manzoni_writer_fiction
				NOR = {
					has_trait = manzoni_genre_adventure
					has_trait = manzoni_genre_crime_mystery
					has_trait = manzoni_genre_devout
					has_trait = manzoni_genre_juvenile
					has_trait = manzoni_genre_literary_fiction
					has_trait = manzoni_genre_romance
					has_trait = manzoni_genre_science_fiction
					has_trait = manzoni_genre_social_critic
				}
			}
			mr_trait_generation_writer_genres_effect = yes
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				has_role = agitator
			}
			remove_character_role = agitator
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_role = general
			}
			remove_character_role = general
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_role = admiral
			}
			remove_character_role = admiral
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_role = politician }
			}
			add_character_role = politician
		}

		writer_experience_set_up_effect = yes
		set_variable = {
			name = mr_is_local_writer_var
			value = root
		}
		place_character_in_void = 1200

		owner = {
			artists_set_up_local_writer_list_effect = yes
		}
	}
}

# Creates a new Writer without losing the old one
#This one was a little harder as the scope was only valid in the random_list
#Therefore a Variable is set to save the scope again. then gets deleted
create_new_writer_effect = {
	random_list = {
		100 = { #Franz Grillparzer, Austrian
			trigger = {
				NOT = { has_global_variable = mr_grillparzer_franz_created_global_var }
				has_state_in_state_region = STATE_AUSTRIA #Born in Vienna
				country_average_cultural_acceptance = {
					target = cu:south_german
					value >= acceptance_status_3
				}
				game_date < 1846.01.15 #Age 55
				year >= 1810 #First few poems, etc. at age 18
			}
			create_character = {
				template = mr_aus_grillparzer_franz_character_template
				save_scope_as = manzoni_new_writer_scope
			}
			scope:manzoni_new_writer_scope = {
				set_variable = mr_is_writer_var
				set_variable = mr_no_headgear_var
				writer_experience_set_up_effect = yes
				place_character_in_void = 1200
			}

			set_variable = {
				name = manzoni_new_writer_var
				value = scope:manzoni_new_writer_scope
			}

			set_global_variable = mr_grillparzer_franz_created_global_var
		}
		100 = { #Franz Kafka, Austrian
			trigger = {
				NOT = { has_global_variable = mr_kafka_created_global_var }
				has_state_in_state_region = STATE_BOHEMIA
				country_average_cultural_acceptance = {
					target = cu:south_german
					value >= acceptance_status_3
				}
				game_date < 1938.7.3 #Age 55
				year >= 1904 #Beschreibung eines Kampfes
			}
			create_character = {
				template = mr_aus_kafka_franz_character_template
				save_scope_as = manzoni_new_writer_scope
			}
			scope:manzoni_new_writer_scope = {
				set_variable = mr_is_writer_var
				set_variable = mr_no_headgear_var
				writer_experience_set_up_effect = yes
				place_character_in_void = 1200
			}

			set_variable = {
				name = manzoni_new_writer_var
				value = scope:manzoni_new_writer_scope
			}

			set_global_variable = mr_kafka_created_global_var
		}
		100 = { #Robert Musil, Austrian
			trigger = {
				NOT = { has_global_variable = mr_musil_created_global_var }
				OR = {
					has_state_in_state_region = STATE_MORAVIA
					has_state_in_state_region = STATE_AUSTRIA
				}

					target = cu:south_german

			}

				set_variable = mr_is_writer_var
				set_variable = mr_no_headgear_var
				writer_experience_set_up_effect = yes
				place_character_in_void = 1200
			}

			set_variable = {
				name = manzoni_new_writer_var
				value = scope:manzoni_new_writer_scope
			}

			set_global_variable = mr_musil_created_global_var

						}
					}
				}
			}
		}

		save_scope_as = manzoni_new_writer_scope
	}

# Set new Writer as official Writer
manzoni_set_new_writer_as_writer_effect = {
	custom_tooltip = {
		text = manzoni_replace_writer_with_new_writer_tt

		#Remove old writer
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = manzoni_writer_var
			}
			var:manzoni_writer_var = {
				free_character_from_void = no
			}
		}
		#Removes Modifier for reading tour
		if = {
			limit = { has_modifier = manzoni_writer_on_tour_modifier }
			remove_modifier = manzoni_writer_on_tour_modifier
		}

		set_variable = {
			name = manzoni_writer_var
			value = scope:manzoni_new_writer_scope
		}

		remove_variable = manzoni_new_writer_var
	}
}

# Remove new Writer
manzoni_remove_new_writer_effect = {
	scope:manzoni_new_writer_scope = {
		free_character_from_void = no
	}

	remove_variable = manzoni_new_writer_var
}

#This effect makes the new writer a local writer
manzoni_set_new_writer_local_writer_effect = {
	custom_tooltip = {
		text = manzoni_set_new_writer_local_writer_tt

		scope:manzoni_new_writer_scope = {
			remove_variable = mr_is_writer_var
			set_variable = {
				name = mr_is_local_writer_var
				value = root
			}
		}
	
		remove_variable = manzoni_new_writer_var
		artists_set_up_local_writer_list_effect = yes
	}
}

#This effect makes the new writer a local writer of another country
manzoni_set_new_writer_local_writer_other_country_effect = {
	custom_tooltip = {
		text = manzoni_set_new_writer_local_writer_other_country_tt

		scope:manzoni_new_writer_scope = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					any_country = {
						country_has_primary_culture = scope:manzoni_new_writer_scope.culture
					}
				}
				random_country = {
					limit = {
						country_has_primary_culture = scope:manzoni_new_writer_scope.culture
					}
					save_scope_as = manzoni_new_country_scope
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					any_country = {
						country_average_cultural_acceptance = {
							target = scope:manzoni_new_writer_scope.culture
							value >= acceptance_status_3
						}
					}
				}
				random_country = {
					limit = {
						country_average_cultural_acceptance = {
							target = scope:manzoni_new_writer_scope.culture
							value >= acceptance_status_3
						}
					}
					save_scope_as = manzoni_new_country_scope
				}
			}
			else = {
				random_country = {
					save_scope_as = manzoni_new_country_scope
				}
			}

			remove_variable = mr_is_writer_var
			set_variable = {
				name = mr_is_local_writer_var
				value = scope:manzoni_new_country_scope
			}
			scope:manzoni_new_country_scope = {
				artists_set_up_local_writer_list_effect = yes
			}
		}
	
		remove_variable = manzoni_new_writer_var
	}
}

# Used to set up the Experience of a character 
writer_experience_set_up_effect = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = {
				has_variable = manzoni_writer_experience
			}
		}
		#Age: 2 Reputation for each year older than 25
		if = {
			limit = {
				age > 25
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = manzoni_writer_experience
				value = age
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = manzoni_writer_experience
				add = -25
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = manzoni_writer_experience
				multiply = 2
			}
		}
		else = {
			set_variable = {
				name = manzoni_writer_experience
				value = 0
			}
		}
		#Random Reputation factor
		set_local_variable = {
			name = random_amount_local_var
			value = { 25 50 }
		}
		change_variable = {
			name = manzoni_writer_experience
			add = local_var:random_amount_local_var
		}
		change_variable = {
			name = manzoni_writer_experience
			add = artists_writer_experience_set_up_value
		}
		if = { #Adds the Great Writer Trait if Experience is above 500
			limit = {
				has_variable = manzoni_writer_experience
				var:manzoni_writer_experience >= 500
				NOT = {
					has_trait = manzoni_great_writer
				}
			}
			remove_trait = literary
			add_trait = manzoni_great_writer
		}
	}

	#Number of Bestsellers
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { has_variable = manzoni_num_bestsellers_var }
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = manzoni_num_bestsellers_var
			value = 0
		}
	}
	#Number of Book Licenses
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { has_variable = manzoni_num_book_licenses_var }
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = manzoni_num_book_licenses_var
			value = 0
		}
	}
	#Number of Book Licenses
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { has_variable = manzoni_num_book_licenses_var }
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = manzoni_num_book_licenses_var
			value = 0
		}
	}
	#Number of Publications
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { has_variable = manzoni_num_publications_var }
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = manzoni_num_publications_var
			value = 0
		}
	}
}

#Writer Experience gain
writer_experience_gain_effect = { #adds XP to the Writer
	# Amount = amount of XP to add
	save_temporary_scope_value_as = { #This is used to display the amount in the tooltip
		name = xp_amount
		value = $AMOUNT$
	}

	if = {
		limit = {
			has_variable = manzoni_writer_var #should only add experience if there actually is a Writer
		}
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = manzoni_writer_experience_gain_tt
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						var:manzoni_writer_var = { #Fallback to make sure there are no errors if the Writer does not have the variable yet
							has_variable = manzoni_writer_experience
						}
					}
				}
				var:manzoni_writer_var = { #Sets the experience in case it was not set yet
					writer_experience_set_up_effect = yes
				}
			}
			var:manzoni_writer_var = {
				change_variable = {
					name = manzoni_writer_experience
					add = $AMOUNT$
				}
				clamp_variable = {
					name = manzoni_writer_experience
					min = 0
					max = 500
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:manzoni_writer_var = {
					var:manzoni_writer_experience >= 500
					NOT = {
						has_trait = manzoni_great_writer
					}
				}
			}
			trigger_event = {
				id = artists.102
				popup = yes
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				var:manzoni_writer_var = {
					remove_trait = literary
					add_trait = manzoni_great_writer
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#Void Writer Experience gain
void_writer_experience_gain_effect = { #adds XP to the Writer
	# Amount = amount of XP to add
	save_temporary_scope_value_as = { #This is used to display the amount in the tooltip
		name = xp_amount
		value = $AMOUNT$
	}
	save_scope_as = manzoni_writer_scope

	custom_tooltip = {
		text = manzoni_void_writer_experience_gain_tt
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_variable = manzoni_writer_experience }
			}
			writer_experience_set_up_effect = yes
		}
		change_variable = {
			name = manzoni_writer_experience
			add = $AMOUNT$
		}
		clamp_variable = {
			name = manzoni_writer_experience
			min = 0
			max = 500
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			var:manzoni_writer_experience >= 500
			NOT = {
				has_trait = manzoni_great_writer
			}
		}
		remove_trait = literary
		add_trait = manzoni_great_writer
	}
}

######Painter######

#This effect kills the current painter
kill_painter_effect = {
	var:klimt_painter_var = {
		free_character_from_void = no
	}

	remove_variable = klimt_painter_var
}

#This effect makes the current painter an independent painter
set_painter_independent_painter_effect = {
	if = {
		limit = { has_variable = klimt_painter_var }

		custom_tooltip = {
			text = set_painter_independent_painter_effect_tt
	
			var:klimt_painter_var = {
				remove_variable = mr_is_painter_var
				set_variable = mr_is_independent_painter
				add_to_global_variable_list = {
					name = mr_independent_painter_global_list
					target = this
				}
			}
		
			remove_variable = klimt_painter_var
		}
	}
}

# Creates a new Painter without losing the old one

#Therefore a Variable is set to save the scope again. then gets deleted

		100 = { #Adolf Hitler, Austria
			trigger = {
				ecchi_r_is_active = no
				NOT = { has_global_variable = mr_hitler_created_global_var }
				has_global_variable = mr_hitler_painter
				has_state_in_state_region = STATE_AUSTRIA
				country_average_cultural_acceptance = {
					target = cu:south_german
					value >= acceptance_status_3
				}
				game_date < 1944.4.20 #Age 55
				year >= 1910 #three years after he failed the entrance exam of the Vienna Arts Academy
			}
			create_character = {
				template = mr_ger_hitler_painter_character_template

				set_variable = mr_is_painter_var
				set_variable = mr_no_headgear_var
				painter_experience_set_up_effect = yes
				place_character_in_void = 1200	
			}

			set_variable = {
				name = klimt_new_painter_var
				value = scope:klimt_new_painter_scope
			}

			set_global_variable = mr_hitler_created_global_var

#Sets an Painter as an independent Painter
gaudi_set_painter_independent_painter = {
	remove_variable = mr_is_painter_var
	set_variable = mr_is_independent_painter

	#Is used to prevent a country from getting that Painter immediately afterwards
	set_variable = {
		name = klimt_painter_unavailable_for_this_var
		value = root
		years = 5
	}

	#Sends the old Painter to the independent Painters
	add_to_global_variable_list = {
		name = mr_independent_painter_global_list
		target = this
	}
}

# Set new Painter as official Painter
klimt_set_new_painter_as_painter_effect = {
	custom_tooltip = {
		text = klimt_replace_painter_with_new_painter_tt
	
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = klimt_painter_var
			}

			var:klimt_painter_var = {
				gaudi_set_painter_independent_painter = yes
			}
		}

		set_variable = {
			name = klimt_painter_var
			value = scope:klimt_new_painter_scope
		}

		remove_variable = klimt_new_painter_var
	}
}

# Set new Painter as independent Painter
klimt_set_new_painter_as_independent_painter_effect = {
	custom_tooltip = {
		text = klimt_set_new_painter_as_independent_painter_effect_tt
	
		add_to_global_variable_list = {
			name = mr_independent_painter_global_list
			target = scope:klimt_new_painter_scope
		}

		scope:klimt_new_painter_scope = {
			gaudi_set_painter_independent_painter = yes
		}

		remove_variable = klimt_new_painter_var
	}
}

# Remove new Painter
klimt_remove_new_painter_effect = {
	scope:klimt_new_painter_scope = {
		free_character_from_void = no
	}

	remove_variable = klimt_new_painter_var
}

# Used to set up the Experience of a character 
painter_experience_set_up_effect = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = {
				has_variable = klimt_painter_experience
			}
		}
		#Age: 5 Reputation per year over 25
		if = {
			limit = {
				age > 25
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = klimt_painter_experience
				value = age
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = klimt_painter_experience
				subtract = 25
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = klimt_painter_experience
				multiply = 5
			}
			if = {
				limit = { var:klimt_painter_experience > 500 }
				set_variable = {
					name = klimt_painter_experience
					value = 500
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			set_variable = {
				name = klimt_painter_experience
				value = 0
			}
		}
		#Random Reputation factor
		set_local_variable = {
			name = random_amount_local_var
			value = { 25 50 }
		}
		change_variable = {
			name = klimt_painter_experience
			add = local_var:random_amount_local_var
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					klimt_has_gallery = yes
				}
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = klimt_painter_experience
				add = 20
			}
		}
		if = { #Adds the Great Painter Trait if Experience is above 500
			limit = {
				var:klimt_painter_experience >= 500
				NOT = {
					has_trait = klimt_great_painter
				}
			}
			remove_trait = klimt_painter
			add_trait = klimt_great_painter
		}
	}
}

#This effect gives special historical characters 250-350 reputation when created
set_historical_painter_experience_effect = {
	set_variable = {
		name = klimt_painter_experience
		value = { 250 350 }
	}
	set_variable = {
		name = klimt_painter_num_paintings_var
		value = { 5 20 }
	}
	set_variable = {
		name = klimt_painter_num_masterworks_var
		value = { 0 3 }
	}
}

#Painter Experience gain
painter_experience_gain_effect = { #adds XP to the Painter
	# Amount = amount of XP to add
	save_temporary_scope_value_as = { #This is used to display the amount in the tooltip
		name = xp_amount
		value = $AMOUNT$
	}

	if = {
		limit = {
			has_variable = klimt_painter_var #should only add experience if there actually is a Painter
		}
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = klimt_painter_experience_gain_tt
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						var:klimt_painter_var = { #Fallback to make sure there are no errors if the Painter does not have the variable yet
							has_variable = klimt_painter_experience
						}
					}
				}
				var:klimt_painter_var = { #Sets the experience in case it was not set yet
					painter_experience_set_up_effect = yes
				}
			}
			var:klimt_painter_var = {
				change_variable = {
					name = klimt_painter_experience
					add = $AMOUNT$
				}
				clamp_variable = {
					name = klimt_painter_experience
					min = 0
					max = 500
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:klimt_painter_var = {
					var:klimt_painter_experience >= 500
					NOT = {
						has_trait = klimt_great_painter
					}
				}
			}
			trigger_event = {
				id = artists.103
				popup = yes
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				var:klimt_painter_var = {
					remove_trait = klimt_painter
					add_trait = klimt_great_painter
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#Effect used to set the cost of the independent painter
#Use it in the character scope with root being a country.
klimt_independent_painter_character_set_up_cost_effect = {
	root = {
		add_treasury = {
			if = {
				limit = { prev.var:klimt_painter_experience > 0 }
				value = prev.var:klimt_painter_experience
				divide = 2
				multiply = money_amount_multiplier_small
				max = {
					value = prev.var:klimt_painter_experience
					multiply = 10000
				}
				multiply = -1
			}
			else = {
				value = 1
				divide = 2
				multiply = money_amount_multiplier_small
				max = 100000
				multiply = -1
			}
		}
	}
}

######Architect######

#This effect kills the current Architect
kill_architect_effect = {
	var:gaudi_architect_var = {
		free_character_from_void = no
	}

	remove_variable = gaudi_architect_var
}

#This effect makes the current Architect an independent Architect
set_architect_independent_architect_effect = {
	if = {
		limit = { has_variable = gaudi_architect_var }

		custom_tooltip = {
			text = set_architect_independent_architect_effect_tt
	
			var:gaudi_architect_var = {
				remove_variable = mr_is_architect_var
				set_variable = mr_is_independent_architect_var
				add_to_global_variable_list = {
					name = mr_independent_architect_global_list
					target = this
				}
			}
		
			remove_variable = gaudi_architect_var
		}
	}
}

# Creates a new Architect without losing the old one
#This one was a little harder as the scope was only valid in the random_list
#Therefore a Variable is set to save the scope again. then gets deleted
create_new_architect_effect = {
	random_list = {
		100 = { #Adolf Loos, Austria
			trigger = {
				NOT = { has_global_variable = mr_loos_adolf_created_global_var }
				OR = {
					has_state_in_state_region = STATE_BOHEMIA #born in Brno
					has_state_in_state_region = STATE_AUSTRIA #Worked in Vienna most of his life
				}
				country_average_cultural_acceptance = {
					target = cu:south_german
					value >= acceptance_status_4
				}
				game_date < 1925.12.10 #Age 55
				year >= 1896 #Started work in Vienna
			}
			create_character = {
				template = mr_aus_loos_adolf_character_template

				save_scope_as = gaudi_new_architect_scope
			}
			scope:gaudi_new_architect_scope = {
				set_variable = mr_is_architect_var #Could be used for clothing or a role in the future
				set_variable = mr_no_headgear_var
				architect_experience_set_up_effect = yes #sets up experience for the character (0 till 30 and then 10 Experience per year)
				place_character_in_void = 1200 #This is needed so the character doesn't disappear
			}

			set_variable = {
				name = gaudi_new_architect_var
				value = scope:gaudi_new_architect_scope
			}

			set_global_variable = mr_loos_adolf_created_global_var #Makes sure the character is not created again
		}
		100 = { #Otto Wagner, Austria
			trigger = {
				NOT = { has_global_variable = mr_wagner_otto_created_global_var }
				has_state_in_state_region = STATE_AUSTRIA #Born and lived in Vienna

							limit = { has_law = law_type:law_women_in_the_workplace }

						}
						if = {

							add = 30
						}
					}
				}
				90 = {
					create_character = {
						age = { 16 30 }
						trait_generation = {}
						save_scope_as = gaudi_new_architect_scope
					}

							limit = { has_law = law_type:law_womens_suffrage }
							add = -30
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

		save_scope_as = gaudi_new_architect_scope
	}

#Sets an architect as an independent Architect
gaudi_set_architect_independent_architect = {
	remove_variable = mr_is_architect_var
	set_variable = mr_is_independent_architect_var

	#Is used to prevent a country from getting that Architect immediately afterwards
	set_variable = {
		name = gaudi_architect_unavailable_for_this_var
		value = root
		years = 5
	}

	#Sends the old Architect to the independent Architects
	add_to_global_variable_list = {
		name = mr_independent_architect_global_list
		target = this
	}
}

# Set new architect as official Architect
gaudi_set_new_architect_as_architect_effect = {
	custom_tooltip = {
		text = gaudi_replace_architect_with_new_architect_tt
	
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = gaudi_architect_var
			}

			var:gaudi_architect_var = {
				gaudi_set_architect_independent_architect = yes
			}
		}

		set_variable = {
			name = gaudi_architect_var
			value = scope:gaudi_new_architect_scope
		}

		remove_variable = gaudi_new_architect_var

		if = {
			limit = { gaudi_has_active_architecture_project_trigger = yes }
			var:gaudi_architect_var = {
				set_character_busy_and_immortal = yes
			}
		}

		#Adds the default Action
		add_journal_entry = {
			type = je_gaudi_public_construction
		}
		je:je_gaudi_public_construction = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = gaudi_architect_public_construction_modifier
				multiplier = gaudi_architect_public_construction_value #Multiplies the base construction (1) with the public construction value
			}
		}
	}
}

# Set new Architect as independent Architect
gaudi_set_new_architect_as_independent_architect_effect = {
	custom_tooltip = {
		text = gaudi_set_new_architect_as_independent_architect_effect_tt

		scope:gaudi_new_architect_scope = {
			gaudi_set_architect_independent_architect = yes
		}

		remove_variable = gaudi_new_architect_var
	}
}

# Remove new Architect
gaudi_remove_new_architect_effect = {
	scope:gaudi_new_architect_scope = {
		free_character_from_void = no
	}

	remove_variable = gaudi_new_architect_var
}

# Used to set up the Experience of a character 
architect_experience_set_up_effect = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = {
				has_variable = gaudi_architect_experience
			}
		}
		#Age: 5 Reputation per year over 25
		if = {
			limit = {
				age > 25
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = gaudi_architect_experience
				value = age
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = gaudi_architect_experience
				subtract = 25
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = gaudi_architect_experience
				multiply = 5
			}
			if = {
				limit = { var:gaudi_architect_experience > 500 }
				set_variable = {
					name = gaudi_architect_experience
					value = 500
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			set_variable = {
				name = gaudi_architect_experience
				value = 0
			}
		}
		#Random Reputation factor
		set_local_variable = {
			name = random_amount_local_var
			value = { 25 50 }
		}
		change_variable = {
			name = gaudi_architect_experience
			add = local_var:random_amount_local_var
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					gaudi_has_architecture_school_trigger = yes
				}
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = gaudi_architect_experience
				add = 20
			}
		}
		if = { #Adds the Great Architect Trait if Experience is above 500
			limit = {
				var:gaudi_architect_experience >= 500
				NOT = {
					has_trait = gaudi_great_architect
				}
			}
			remove_trait = gaudi_architect
			add_trait = gaudi_great_architect
		}
	}
}

#This effect gives special historical characters 250-350 reputation when created
set_historical_architect_experience_effect = {
	set_variable = {
		name = gaudi_architect_experience
		value = { 250 350 }
	}
}

#Architect Experience gain
architect_experience_gain_effect = { #adds XP to the Architect
	# Amount = amount of XP to add
	save_temporary_scope_value_as = { #This is used to display the amount in the tooltip
		name = xp_amount
		value = $AMOUNT$
	}

	if = {
		limit = {
			has_variable = gaudi_architect_var #should only add experience if there actually is a Architect
		}
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = gaudi_architect_experience_gain_tt
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						var:gaudi_architect_var = { #Fallback to make sure there are no errors if the Architect does not have the variable yet
							has_variable = gaudi_architect_experience
						}
					}
				}
				var:gaudi_architect_var = { #Sets the experience in case it was not set yet
					architect_experience_set_up_effect = yes
				}
			}
			var:gaudi_architect_var = {
				change_variable = {
					name = gaudi_architect_experience
					add = $AMOUNT$
				}
				clamp_variable = {
					name = gaudi_architect_experience
					min = 0
					max = 500
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:gaudi_architect_var = {
					var:gaudi_architect_experience >= 500
					NOT = {
						has_trait = gaudi_great_architect
					}
				}
			}
			trigger_event = {
				id = artists.104
				popup = yes
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				var:gaudi_architect_var = {
					remove_trait = gaudi_architect
					add_trait = gaudi_great_architect
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

######Biennale######

#Give the three countries with most artist reputation a prize
artists_biennale_winner_effect = {
	#Removes the GLOBAL ranking variables
	remove_global_variable = artists_biennale_place_1_global_var 
	remove_global_variable = artists_biennale_place_2_global_var 
	remove_global_variable = artists_biennale_place_3_global_var 

	ordered_country = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_technology_researched = elgar_impressionism_tech
				has_technology_researched = elgar_expressionism_tech
				has_technology_researched = elgar_art_nouveau_tech
				NOT = {
					has_modifier = artists_biennale_triumph_modifier
				}
			}
		}
		order_by = artists_biennale_value
		max = 3 #Limits the list to the three top countries
		check_range_bounds = no #prevents errors

		#This part checks one after another whether the the first, second, etc. ranked countries are saved already.
		#Luckily the ordered_country effect iterates through the countries one after another.
		#So the first country gets saved to the first variable but as that variable now is set,
		# the second country gets saved to the second variable and so on.
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { 
					has_global_variable = artists_biennale_place_1_global_var  
				}
			}
			set_global_variable = {
				name = artists_biennale_place_1_global_var  
				value = this
			}
			save_scope_as = artists_biennale_first_winner_scope
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_global_variable = artists_biennale_place_2_global_var   }
			}
			set_global_variable = {
				name = artists_biennale_place_2_global_var 
				value = this
			}
			save_scope_as = artists_biennale_second_winner_scope
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_global_variable = artists_biennale_place_3_global_var   }
			}
			set_global_variable = {
				name = artists_biennale_place_3_global_var 
				value = this
			}
			save_scope_as = artists_biennale_third_winner_scope
		}
	}
}

#This effect gives starter characters some random stats
set_start_painter_stats_effect = {
	set_variable = {
		name = klimt_painter_num_paintings_var
		value = { 1 10 }

	set_variable = {
		name = klimt_painter_num_masterworks_var
		value = 0
	}
}

	remove_variable = artists_promote_writer_active_var
	remove_variable = artists_promote_painter_active_var
	remove_variable = artists_promote_architect_active_var
	remove_variable = artists_promotion_active
}
